- Decode text/plain attachments.
- Replace binary attachments with metadata placeholders.

[MODEL] ### 📋 Execution Plan

1. **Authentication:** 
   - Dynamically request GCP credentials token using `gcloud auth print-access-token`.
   - Fall back to `gcloud auth application-default print-access-token`.
   - Handle login failures by prompting appropriate authentication commands.

2. **GCP Dataset Pull:**
   - Construct the REST URL pointing to the Vertex AI Dataset API endpoint representing the saved prompt:
     `https://us-central1-aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/{project}/locations/{location}/datasets/{prompt_id}`
   - Pull the raw dataset JSON using Python's standard `urllib.request` library (no external HTTP library dependency).

3. **Deterministic Prompt Extraction:**
   - Recursively parse the raw JSON to look for `system_instruction` / `systemInstruction` and `contents` / `prompt_message`.
   - Crawl any stringified inner JSON under `metadata.text` to guarantee absolute coverage of modern Vertex Studio structures.
   - Fall back to a generalized text crawler if structured fields are absent.

4. **Attachment Decoder & Stripper:**
   - **Text attachments (`text/plain`):** Detect and decode base64 inline content to plain-text string.
   - **Binary attachments (Images/PDFs/Videos):** Safe-strip raw base64 data to metadata placeholder templates (`[Binary Attachment: image/png, size: X bytes]`) to avoid corrupting prompt context.
   - **Remote GCS references:** Convert into human-readable reference tags.

5. **Prompt Packaging:**
   - Create local structure under `saved_prompts/{prompt_id}/`.
   - Save the raw JSON, system instructions, extracted content, chunks, final assembled prompt, `master.md` runner, and `index.json` summary block.

6. **Aider Triggering:**
   - Call `./start_aider.sh gemini-flash saved_prompts/<prompt_id>/master.md` dynamically with stderr/stdout streaming in real-time.

### 📂 File Artifacts

#### 1. Python Agent (`agents/prompt_id_coder_agent.py`)

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Prompt-ID Coding Agent
Fetches saved prompts from Google Cloud Vertex AI Dataset API,
extracts and decodes contents, builds a local prompt package,
and automatically triggers Aider to perform the coding task.
"""

import os
import sys
import argparse
import json
import base64
import subprocess
import urllib.request
import urllib.error
import ssl
from datetime import datetime

# Configure logging
def log_info(msg):
    print(f"INFO: {msg}")

def log_success(msg):
    print(f"🟢 SUCCESS: {msg}")

def log_warning(msg):
    print(f"⚠️ WARNING: {msg}")

def log_error(msg):
    print(f"❌ ERROR: {msg}", file=sys.stderr)


def get_gcloud_config(key):
    """
    Retrieves a gcloud configuration value.
    """
    try:
        res = subprocess.run(
            ["gcloud", "config", "get-value", key],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )
        val = res.stdout.strip()
        if val and "(unset)" not in val:
            return val
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None


def get_access_token():
    """
    Attempts to retrieve active Google Cloud credentials token.
    First tries standard auth print-access-token,
    then falls back to application-default print-access-token.
    If both fail, prints instructions.
    """
    # 1. Try standard print-access-token
    try:
        res = subprocess.run(
            ["gcloud", "auth", "print-access-token"],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )
        token = res.stdout.strip()
        if token:
            log_success("Acquired active gcloud session access token.")
            return token
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 2. Try application-default print-access-token
    try:
        res = subprocess.run(
            ["gcloud", "auth", "application-default", "print-access-token"],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )
        token = res.stdout.strip()
        if token:
            log_success("Acquired Application Default Credentials access token.")
            return token
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 3. Both failed
    log_error("Failed to acquire access token. Authentication is required.")
    print("\nPlease login using the following commands:")
    print("  gcloud auth login --no-launch-browser")
    print("  gcloud auth application-default login --no-launch-browser")
    print("  gcloud config set project ctoteam\n")
    sys.exit(1)


def fetch_prompt_dataset(project, location, prompt_id, token):
    """
    Fetches the raw prompt dataset JSON from Vertex AI Dataset API.
    """
    url = f"https://{location}-aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/{project}/locations/{location}/datasets/{prompt_id}"
    log_info(f"Fetching dataset resource: {url}")
    
    req = urllib.request.Request(url)
    req.add_header("Authorization", f"Bearer {token}")
    req.add_header("Content-Type", "application/json")
    
    context = ssl.create_default_context()
    
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, context=context) as response:
            body = response.read().decode("utf-8")
            return json.loads(body)
    except urllib.error.HTTPError as e:
        body = e.read().decode("utf-8") if e.fp else ""
        log_error(f"HTTP Error {e.code}: {e.reason}")
        if body:
            try:
                err_json = json.loads(body)
                print(json.dumps(err_json, indent=2), file=sys.stderr)
            except Exception:
                print(body, file=sys.stderr)
        raise RuntimeError(f"GCP API returned HTTP {e.code}")
    except Exception as e:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to connect to GCP API: {e}")


def parse_parts(parts_list):
    """
    Parses a list of parts from a content turn, decoding base64 plain-text
    and replacing binary data (image, pdf) with placeholders.
    """
    text_parts = []
    attachments_summary = []
    
    for part in parts_list:
        if not isinstance(part, dict):
            continue
            
        # 1. Plain text parts
        if "text" in part:
            text_parts.append(part["text"])
            
        # 2. Inline base64 data (multimodal prompts)
        elif "inline_data" in part or "inlineData" in part:
            inline_data = part.get("inline_data") or part.get("inlineData", {})
            mime_type = inline_data.get("mime_type") or inline_data.get("mimeType", "")
            base64_data = inline_data.get("data", "")
            
            if "text/plain" in mime_type:
                try:
                    decoded_bytes = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
                    decoded_text = decoded_bytes.decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
                    text_parts.append(decoded_text)
                    attachments_summary.append({
                        "type": "text/plain",
                        "status": "decoded",
                        "size_bytes": len(decoded_bytes)
                    })
                except Exception as e:
                    text_parts.append(f"\n[Error decoding text/plain base64 attachment: {e}]\n")
            else:
                # Strip binary payloads (images, video, PDFs) into metadata placeholders
                size_estimate = (len(base64_data) * 3) // 4 if base64_data else 0
                placeholder = f"\n[Binary Attachment: {mime_type}, size: {size_estimate} bytes]\n"
                text_parts.append(placeholder)
                attachments_summary.append({
                    "type": mime_type,
                    "status": "stripped_to_placeholder",
                    "size_bytes": size_estimate
                })
                
        # 3. Remote files (GCS uris)
        elif "file_data" in part or "fileData" in part:
            file_data = part.get("file_data") or part.get("fileData", {})
            file_uri = file_data.get("file_uri") or file_data.get("fileUri", "")
            mime_type = file_data.get("mime_type") or file_data.get("mimeType", "")
            placeholder = f"\n[GCS File Attachment: {file_uri} (mime: {mime_type})]\n"
            text_parts.append(placeholder)
            attachments_summary.append({
                "type": f"file_data_{mime_type}",
                "status": "placeholder",
                "uri": file_uri
            })
            
    return "\n".join(text_parts), attachments_summary


def find_system_instruction(data):
    """
    Recursively scans JSON object to find system_instruction or systemInstruction.
    """
    if isinstance(data, dict):
        for k, v in data.items():
            if k.lower() in ("system_instruction", "systeminstruction"):
                return v
            res = find_system_instruction(v)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    elif isinstance(data, list):
        for item in data:
            res = find_system_instruction(item)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    return None


def find_contents(data):
    """
    Recursively scans JSON object to find contents or prompt_message parts.
    """
    if isinstance(data, dict):
        for k, v in data.items():
            if k.lower() in ("contents", "prompt_message", "promptmessage"):
                return v
        for k, v in data.items():
            res = find_contents(v)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    elif isinstance(data, list):
        for item in data:
            res = find_contents(item)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    return None


def find_model_reference(data):
    """
    Recursively scans JSON object to find model reference information.
    """
    if isinstance(data, dict):
        for k, v in data.items():
            if k.lower() in ("model", "modelreference", "model_reference"):
                if isinstance(v, str):
                    return v
            res = find_model_reference(v)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    elif isinstance(data, list):
        for item in data:
            res = find_model_reference(item)
            if res is not None:
                return res
    return None


def extract_all_text_parts_fallback(data):
    """
    Fallback crawler to extract any and all text elements from the JSON structure
    if structured contents couldn't be cleanly parsed.
    """
    texts = []
    if isinstance(data, dict):
        if "text" in data and isinstance(data["text"], str):
            try:
                parsed = json.loads(data["text"])
                if isinstance(parsed, (dict, list)):
                    texts.extend(extract_all_text_parts_fallback(parsed))
                    return texts
            except Exception:
                pass
            texts.append(data["text"])
        else:
            for k, v in data.items():
                texts.extend(extract_all_text_parts_fallback(v))
    elif isinstance(data, list):
        for item in data:
            texts.extend(extract_all_text_parts_fallback(item))
    return texts


def parse_system_instruction(sys_inst):
    """
    Extracts plain text from system instruction node.
    """
    if not sys_inst:
        return "", []
    if isinstance(sys_inst, str):
        return sys_inst, []
    if isinstance(sys_inst, dict):
        if "parts" in sys_inst:
            return parse_parts(sys_inst["parts"])
        if "text" in sys_inst:
            return sys_inst["text"], []
    if isinstance(sys_inst, list):
        return parse_parts(sys_inst)
    return str(sys_inst), []


def extract_prompt_data(raw_json):
    """
    Deterministic prompt extraction from Vertex AI Dataset resource JSON.
    """
    system_instruction = ""
    user_content = ""
    model_name = ""
    attachments = []
    
    # Resolve inner metadata
    metadata = raw_json.get("metadata", {})
    inner_data = {}
    
    if isinstance(metadata, dict) and "text" in metadata:
        text_val = metadata["text"]
        if isinstance(text_val, str) and text_val.strip().startswith("{"):
            try:
                inner_data = json.loads(text_val)
            except Exception:
                user_content = text_val
        elif isinstance(text_val, dict):
            inner_data = text_val
        elif isinstance(text_val, str):
            user_content = text_val
    elif isinstance(metadata, dict):
        inner_data = metadata
        
    combined_context = [inner_data, raw_json]
    
    # Extract system instruction
    sys_inst_node = None
    for ctx in combined_context:
        sys_inst_node = find_system_instruction(ctx)
        if sys_inst_node:
            break
            
    if sys_inst_node:
        system_instruction, sys_attachments = parse_system_instruction(sys_inst_node)
        attachments.extend(sys_attachments)
        
    # Extract contents/messages
    contents_node = None
    for ctx in combined_context:
        contents_node = find_contents(ctx)
        if contents_node:
            break
            
    if contents_node:
        content_texts = []
        if isinstance(contents_node, list):
            for turn in contents_node:
                if not isinstance(turn, dict):
                    continue
                role = turn.get("role", "user")
                parts = turn.get("parts", [])
                parsed_text, turn_attachments = parse_parts(parts)
                attachments.extend(turn_attachments)
                
                if role == "user":
                    content_texts.append(parsed_text)
                else:
                    content_texts.append(f"### {role.capitalize()}:\n{parsed_text}")
            user_content = "\n\n".join(content_texts)
        elif isinstance(contents_node, dict):
            if "parts" in contents_node:
                parsed_text, turn_attachments = parse_parts(contents_node["parts"])
                attachments.extend(turn_attachments)
                user_content = parsed_text
            elif "text" in contents_node:
                user_content = contents_node["text"]
        elif isinstance(contents_node, str):
            user_content = contents_node
            
    # Fallback to general crawling if empty
    if not user_content.strip():
        fallback_texts = []
        for ctx in combined_context:
            fallback_texts.extend(extract_all_text_parts_fallback(ctx))
        unique_texts = []
        for t in fallback_texts:
            if t.strip() and t.strip() != system_instruction.strip() and t not in unique_texts:
                unique_texts.append(t)
        if unique_texts:
            user_content = "\n\n".join(unique_texts)
            
    # Extract Model Name
    for ctx in combined_context:
                 role = turn.get("role", "user")
                parts = turn.get("parts", [])
                parsed_text, turn_attachments = parse_parts(parts)
                attachments.extend(turn_attachments)
                
                if role == "user":
                    content_texts.append(parsed_text)
                else:
                    content_texts.append(f"### {role.capitalize()}:\n{parsed_text}")
            user_content = "\n\n".join(content_texts)
        elif isinstance(contents_node, dict):
            if "parts" in contents_node:
                parsed_text, turn_attachments = parse_parts(contents_node["parts"])
                attachments.extend(turn_attachments)
                user_content = parsed_text
            elif "text" in contents_node:
                user_content = contents_node["text"]
        elif isinstance(contents_node, str):
            user_content = contents_node
            
    # Fallback to general crawling if empty
    if not user_content.strip():
        fallback_texts = []
        for ctx in combined_context:
            fallback_texts.extend(extract_all_text_parts_fallback(ctx))
        unique_texts = []
        for t in fallback_texts:
            if t.strip() and t.strip() != system_instruction.strip() and t not in unique_texts:
                unique_texts.append(t)
        if unique_texts:
            user_content = "\n\n".join(unique_texts)
            
    # Extract Model Name
    for ctx in combined_context:
        model_name = find_model_reference(ctx)
        if model_name:
            if "/" in model_name:
                model_name = model_name.split("/")[-1]
            break
            
    if not model_name:
        model_name = raw_json.get("modelReference", "gemini-1.5-flash-002")
        if "/" in model_name:
            model_name = model_name.split("/")[-1]
            
    return system_instruction.strip(), user_content.strip(), model_name.strip(), attachments


def create_local_prompt_package(prompt_id, raw_json, system_instruction, user_content, model_name, attachments):
    """
    Prepares directories and saves the prompt artifacts.
    """
    out_dir = os.path.join("saved_prompts", prompt_id)
    os.makedirs(out_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    # 1. Save raw JSON
    raw_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "raw.json")
    with open(raw_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(raw_json, f, indent=2)
    log_info(f"Saved raw JSON to {raw_path}")
    
    # 2. Save system.md
    sys_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "system.md")
    with open(sys_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(system_instruction)
    log_info(f"Saved system.md to {sys_path}")
    
    # 3. Save extracted_content.txt
    ext_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "extracted_content.txt")
    with open(ext_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(user_content)
    log_info(f"Saved extracted_content.txt to {ext_path}")
    
    # 4. Save chunk_001.md (user prompt template)
    chunk_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "chunk_001.md")
    with open(chunk_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(user_content)
    log_info(f"Saved chunk_001.md to {chunk_path}")
    
    # 5. Save final_assembled.md (combined system instructions and user prompt text)
    assembled_content = f"# System Instruction\n\n{system_instruction}\n\n" \
                        f"--------------------------------------------------\n\n" \
                        f"# User Prompt\n\n{user_content}"
    final_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "final_assembled.md")
    with open(final_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(assembled_content)
    log_info(f"Saved final_assembled.md to {final_path}")
    
    # 6. Save master.md (the primary runner instruction file for Aider)
    master_content = f"""# SYSTEM INSTRUCTIONS
{system_instruction or "You are an expert enterprise software engineering agent."}

# USER PROMPT TASK
{user_content}
"""
    master_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "master.md")
    with open(master_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(master_content)
    log_success(f"Assembled master.md prompt package at {master_path}")
    
    # 7. Save index.json
    index_data = {
        "prompt_id": prompt_id,
        "display_name": raw_json.get("displayName", "Unnamed Prompt"),
        "model_name": model_name,
        "create_time": raw_json.get("createTime", datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"),
        "update_time": raw_json.get("updateTime", datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"),
        "system_instruction_length": len(system_instruction),
        "user_content_length": len(user_content),
        "attachments_summary": attachments
    }
    index_path = os.path.join(out_dir, "index.json")
    with open(index_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(index_data, f, indent=2)
    log_info(f"Saved index.json summary to {index_path}")
    
    return master_path


def run_aider_process(prompt_id):
    """
    Executes the start_aider.sh shell script with the master.md prompt.
    """
    master_path = os.path.join("saved_prompts", prompt_id, "master.md")
    if not os.path.exists(master_path):
        log_error(f"Cannot run Aider: master.md does not exist at {master_path}")
        sys.exit(1)
        
    aider_script = "./start_aider.sh"
    if not os.path.exists(aider_script):
        # Check parent directory as fallback
        if os.path.exists("../start_aider.sh"):
            aider_script = "../start_aider.sh"
        else:
            log_error("Could not locate start_aider.sh script.")
            sys.exit(1)
            
    log_info(f"Executing: {aider_script} gemini-flash {master_path}")
    try:
        subprocess.run([aider_script, "gemini-flash", master_path], check=True)
        log_success("Aider execution finished successfully.")
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        log_error(f"start_aider.sh failed with exit code {e.returncode}")
        sys.exit(e.returncode)
    except Exception as e:
        log_error(f"Unexpected error executing Aider script: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="PRISM Prompt-ID Coding Agent")
    parser.add_argument("--prompt-id", required=True, help="Saved Prompt ID from Vertex AI Dataset")
    parser.add_argument("--project", help="GCP Project ID (defaults to active gcloud config or 'ctoteam')")
    parser.add_argument("--location", help="GCP Location (defaults to active gcloud config or 'us-central1')")
    parser.add_argument("--run-aider", action="store_true", help="Launch start_aider.sh after preparing package")
    
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    # Auto-detect config parameters
    project = args.project or get_gcloud_config("project") or "ctoteam"
    location = args.location or get_gcloud_config("compute/region") or get_gcloud_config("aiplatform/location") or "us-central1"
    prompt_id = args.prompt_id
    
    log_info(f"Configuration: Project={project}, Location={location}, PromptID={prompt_id}")
    
    # Obtain access token safely
    token = get_access_token()
    
    # Fetch prompt dataset from Vertex AI API
    try:
        raw_json = fetch_prompt_dataset(project, location, prompt_id, token)
    except Exception as e:
        log_error(f"Failed to fetch prompt: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)
        
    # Extract structured prompt parts deterministically
    try:
        system_instruction, user_content, model_name, attachments = extract_prompt_data(raw_json)
        log_success("Successfully extracted and decoded prompt data.")
        log_info(f"Model specified in prompt resource: {model_name}")
        log_info(f"System instruction length: {len(system_instruction)} chars")
        log_info(f"User content length: {len(user_content)} chars")
        if attachments:
            log_info(f"Processed {len(attachments)} attachments:")
            for att in attachments:
                log_info(f"  - [{att['status'].upper()}] {att['type']} ({att.get('size_bytes', 0)} bytes)")
    except Exception as e:
        log_error(f"Failed to parse and extract prompt: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)
        
    # Save prepared files locally
    try:
        master_path = create_local_prompt_package(
            prompt_id=prompt_id,
            raw_json=raw_json,
            system_instruction=system_instruction,
            user_content=user_content,
            model_name=model_name,
            attachments=attachments
        )
    except Exception as e:
        log_error(f"Failed to create prompt package: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)
        
    # Trigger Aider execution if requested
    if args.run_aider:
        run_aider_process(prompt_id)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

#### 2. Shell Wrapper (`scripts/run_prompt_id.sh`)

```bash
#!/bin/bash
set -e

# Prompt-ID Coding Agent Bash Runner

PROMPT_ID=$1

if [ -z "$PROMPT_ID" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <prompt_id>"
    echo "Example: $0 2114685765899255808"
    exit 1
fi

# Get the script directory and go to project root
SCRIPT_DIR="$( cd "$( dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}" )" &> /dev/null && pwd )"
cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/.."

echo "--------------------------------------------------"
echo "PRISM Coder Agent: Running Prompt ID: $PROMPT_ID"
echo "--------------------------------------------------"

python3 agents/prompt_id_coder_agent.py --prompt-id "$PROMPT_ID" --run-aider
```

#### 3. README Details (`README.md`)

```markdown
# Prompt-ID Coding Agent

A reusable, VM-based coding agent that accepts any Google Agent Platform / Vertex AI Studio saved prompt ID, pulls the prompt from GCP Vertex AI Dataset API, extracts and decodes its contents deterministically, structures it locally into a prompt package, and launches Aider automatically to execute the coding task.

## Directory Structure

```text
/home/appadmin/projects/Ram_Projects/DiracDelta/coder
├── agents/
│   └── prompt_id_coder_agent.py
├── scripts/
│   └── run_prompt_id.sh
├── saved_prompts/
│   └── <prompt_id>/
│       ├── raw.json
│       ├── system.md
│       ├── extracted_content.txt
│       ├── chunk_001.md
│       ├── final_assembled.md
│       ├── master.md
│       └── index.json
└── README.md
```

## Quick Start

### 1. Authenticate with GCP
Ensure you are logged into gcloud with appropriate permissions to access Vertex AI datasets:
```bash
gcloud auth login --no-launch-browser
gcloud auth application-default login --no-launch-browser
gcloud config set project ctoteam
```

### 2. Run the Agent
Run the agent using the simple shell command:
```bash
./scripts/run_prompt_id.sh <prompt_id>
```

Alternatively, invoke via Python CLI:
```bash
python3 agents/prompt_id_coder_agent.py --prompt-id <prompt_id> --run-aider
```

## How It Works

1. **GCP Token Retrieval:** Dynamically retrieves active gcloud credentials (`gcloud auth print-access-token`), falling back to Application Default Credentials.
2. **Deterministic Fetching:** Queries the Vertex AI Datasets API for the requested `prompt_id`.
3. **Resilient Crawling & Extraction:** Deterministically extracts system instructions and prompt contents by crawling the returned JSON. Supports stringified inner JSON.
4. **Multimodal / Attachment Handling:** Decodes base64-encoded `text/plain` attachments while safely stripping binary/image/pdf payloads into size-labeled placeholders.
5. **Aider Automation:** Launches `start_aider.sh` automatically with the assembled `master.md` prompt.

### Execution Script

Run the following commands in your shell to clean the SQL file and execute the BigQuery schema definition:

```bash
cd /home/appadmin/projects/Ram_Projects/DiracDelta/gcloud_run

cat << 'EOF' > clean_sql.py
import os
import re
import sys
import subprocess

sql_path = "sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql"
print(f"Reading {sql_path}...")

with open(sql_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    sql = f.read()

# 1. Handle location inconsistencies (align us-central1 with the US execution region)
sql = re.sub(r'OPTIONS\s*\(\s*location\s*=\s*[\'"]us-central1[\'"]\s*\)', 'OPTIONS(location="US")', sql, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
sql = re.sub(r'OPTIONS\s*\(\s*location\s*=\s*[\'"]us[\'"]\s*\)', 'OPTIONS(location="US")', sql, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

# 2. Identify and clean each table body definition
def clean_table_body(body):
    lines = body.splitlines()
    cleaned_lines = []
    
    for line in lines:
        stripped = line.strip()
        if not stripped:
            cleaned_lines.append(line)
            continue
            
        is_constraint = False
        upper_stripped = stripped.upper()
        if (upper_stripped.startswith("CONSTRAINT") or 
            upper_stripped.startswith("PRIMARY KEY") or 
            upper_stripped.startswith("FOREIGN KEY") or 
            upper_stripped.startswith("UNIQUE") or 
            upper_stripped.startswith("CHECK")):
            is_constraint = True
            
        if is_constraint:
            # Comment out constraint to keep documentation/intent intact
            cleaned_lines.append("  -- " + stripped)
            continue
            
        cleaned_line = line
        
        # Remove DEFAULT clauses
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+DEFAULT\s+CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\(\)", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+DEFAULT\s+(FALSE|TRUE)", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+DEFAULT\s+'[^']*'", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r'\s+DEFAULT\s+"[^"]*"', "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+DEFAULT\s+\d+", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+DEFAULT\s+[a-zA-Z0-9_().]+", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        
        # Remove column-level UNIQUE, PRIMARY KEY, and AUTO_INCREMENT clauses
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+UNIQUE", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+PRIMARY\s+KEY", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        cleaned_line = re.sub(r"\s+AUTO_INCREMENT", "", cleaned_line, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
        
        cleaned_lines.append(cleaned_line)
        
    # Remove trailing comma from the last active column of the table block
    last_active_idx = -1
    for i in range(len(cleaned_lines) - 1, -1, -1):
        line_stripped = cleaned_lines[i].strip()
        if line_stripped and not line_stripped.startswith("--"):
            last_active_idx = i
            break
            
    if last_active_idx != -1:
        line = cleaned_lines[last_active_idx]
        if " --" in line:
            parts = line.split(" --", 1)
            left = parts[0].rstrip()
            if left.endswith(","):
                left = left[:-1].rstrip()
            cleaned_lines[last_active_idx] = f"{left} --{parts[1]}"
        elif " #" in line:
            parts = line.split(" #", 1)
            left = parts[0].rstrip()
            if left.endswith(","):
                left = left[:-1].rstrip()
            cleaned_lines[last_active_idx] = f"{left} #{parts[1]}"
        else:
            left = line.rstrip()
            if left.endswith(","):
                cleaned_lines[last_active_idx] = left[:-1]
                
    return "\n".join(cleaned_lines)

# Apply global table cleanups
def replacer(match):
    prefix = match.group(1)
    body = match.group(2)
    suffix = match.group(3)
    return prefix + clean_table_body(body) + suffix

cleaned_sql = re.sub(
    r'(CREATE\s+TABLE\s+(?:IF\s+NOT\s+EXISTS\s+)?[\w.]+\s*\()(.*?)(\))',
    replacer,
    sql,
    flags=re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL
)

with open(sql_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(cleaned_sql)

print(f"Successfully cleaned and updated {sql_path}.")

# Check if active DEFAULT or relational constraints are present
print("\nChecking for remaining active DEFAULT or constraint clauses:")
res_grep = subprocess.run(
    "grep -vE '^\s*--' sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql | grep -nE 'DEFAULT|UNIQUE|PRIMARY KEY|FOREIGN KEY|REFERENCES|CHECK' || true",
    shell=True,
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)
print(res_grep.stdout)

# Rerun the BigQuery DDL query to verify
print("Executing BigQuery DDL query...")
res_bq = subprocess.run(
    "bq query --use_legacy_sql=false < sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql",
    shell=True,
    capture_output=True,
    text=True
)
print("STDOUT:")
print(res_bq.stdout)
print("STDERR:")
print(res_bq.stderr)

if res_bq.returncode != 0:
    print("❌ BigQuery DDL Query FAILED!")
    sys.exit(res_bq.returncode)
else:
    print("🟢 BigQuery DDL Query SUCCEEDED!")
EOF

python3 clean_sql.py
rm clean_sql.py
```

[MODEL] The issue occurs because the `OPTIONS(...)` block spans multiple lines with multiple fields (`description="..."` and `location="us-central1"`), which prevented the single-line regex from matching.

Replacing all occurrences of `location="us-central1"` with `location="US"` globally will solve this perfectly.

Run the following command to apply the fix and execute the query:

```bash
cd /home/appadmin/projects/Ram_Projects/DiracDelta/gcloud_run

python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
import re

p = Path("sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql")
s = p.read_text()

# Globally align location with the active execution region
s = re.sub(r'location\s*=\s*[\'"]us-central1[\'"]', 'location="US"', s, flags=re.IGNORECASE)

p.write_text(s)
print("Updated us-central1 location constraints to US")
PY

# Verify no remaining us-central1 specifications
grep -ni "us-central1" sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql || true

# Execute the updated DDL query
bq query --use_legacy_sql=false < sql/prompt_catalog/create_tables.sql
```

#!/bin/bash
# Extract and Store Prompt in GCS + BigQuery Catalog
# Usage: ./scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh <prompt_id> [--force]

set -euo pipefail

SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
PROJECT_ROOT="$(cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/.." && pwd)"

cd "$PROJECT_ROOT"

PROMPT_ID="${1:?ERROR: prompt_id required}"
FORCE="${2:-}"

echo "=============================================================="
echo "EXTRACT & STORE PROMPT TO GCS + BigQuery"
echo "=============================================================="
echo "Prompt ID: $PROMPT_ID"
echo "Project: ctoteam"
echo "Bucket: gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/"
echo ""

# STAGE 1: Extract & Upload to GCS
echo "[STAGE 1] Extracting and uploading to GCS..."
METADATA_JSON=$(python3 agents/gcs_prompt_store.py \
 --prompt-id "$PROMPT_ID" \
 --project-id "ctoteam" \
 --location "us-central1" \
 --bucket "agentproject" \
 $([[ -n "$FORCE" ]] && echo "--force") 2>&1 | tail -50)

# Extract run_id from metadata
RUN_ID=$(echo "$METADATA_JSON" | jq -r '.run_id')

if [[ -z "$RUN_ID" || "$RUN_ID" == "null" ]]; then
 echo "ERROR: Failed to extract run_id from metadata"
 exit 1
fi

echo "✓ Uploaded to GCS (run_id: ${RUN_ID:0:8}...)"

# STAGE 2: Register in BigQuery
echo ""
echo "[STAGE 2] Registering in BigQuery catalog..."

RUN_FOLDER="$PROJECT_ROOT/saved_prompts/$PROMPT_ID/runs/$RUN_ID"

python3 agents/bigquery_prompt_catalog.py \
 --prompt-id "$PROMPT_ID" \
 --run-id "$RUN_ID" \
 --project-id "ctoteam" \
 --run-folder "$RUN_FOLDER"

echo ""
echo "=============================================================="
echo "EXTRACTION COMPLETE"
echo "=============================================================="
echo ""
echo "GCS Location:"
echo " gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/$PROMPT_ID/runs/$RUN_ID/"
echo ""
echo "Query Latest Extractions:"
echo " bq query --use_legacy_sql=false '"
echo "  SELECT prompt_id, run_id, chunk_count, user_message_count"
echo "  FROM ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.latest_runs"
echo "  WHERE prompt_id = \"$PROMPT_ID\""
echo "  ORDER BY created_at DESC;"
echo " '"
echo ""
echo "View Run Metadata:"
echo " gsutil cat gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/$PROMPT_ID/latest.json"
echo ""

 #!/usr/bin/env python3
 """
 GCS Prompt Store Agent

 Extracts Vertex AI saved prompts and stores artifacts in Google Cloud Storage.
 Organized by prompt_id and run_id (UUID). Immutable run folders.

 Flow:
 1. Fetch prompt from Vertex AI Dataset API
 2. Extract: system, user messages, attachments (deterministic, no LLM)
 3. Create local run folder: saved_prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
 4. Upload entire run folder to: gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
 5. Update latest.json pointer
 6. Return metadata for BigQuery registration
 """

 import sys
 import json
 import subprocess
 import requests
 import base64
 import argparse
 import hashlib
 import uuid
 from pathlib import Path
 from datetime import datetime
 from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
 from google.cloud import storage

 def get_auth_token() -> str:
   """Get GCP access token."""
   try:
     return subprocess.check_output(
       ["gcloud", "auth", "print-access-token"], text=True
     ).strip()
   except:
     try:
       return subprocess.check_output(
         ["gcloud", "auth", "application-default", "print-access-token"], text=True
       ).strip()
     except:
       print("ERROR: gcloud auth failed. Run: gcloud auth login --no-launch-browser")
       sys.exit(1)


 def compute_md5(data: dict) -> str:
   """Compute MD5 hash of JSON (deterministic)."""
   json_str = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True, separators=(',', ':'))
   return hashlib.md5(json_str.encode()).hexdigest()


 def fetch_prompt(project_id: str, location: str, prompt_id: str, token: str) -> dict:
   """Fetch saved prompt from Vertex AI Dataset API."""
   url = f"https://{location}-aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/{project_id}/locations/
 {location}/datasets/{prompt_id}"
   headers = {
     "Authorization": f"Bearer {token}",
     "x-goog-user-project": project_id,
     "Content-Type": "application/json",
   }

My refined regex approach for `run_id` extraction proved successful. I've now integrated a Python one-liner into `scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh` using `re.DOTALL` for robust, nested JSON handling. This also required modifying `agents/gcs_prompt_store.py` for timezone-aware datetime operations.

**Updating Code Safely**

I'm now writing a Python script to perform the necessary code modifications across `agents/gcs_prompt_store.py` and `scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh`. This ensures that the timezone updates and any other required changes are applied consistently and safely.



[MODEL] To fix the `jq` parse error and prevent python deprecation warnings from corrupting the captured JSON string, we will implement two high-precision modifications:

1. **Suppression of Python Deprecation Warnings:** Replace deprecated, naive `datetime.utcnow()` with modern, timezone-aware `datetime.now(timezone.utc)` in the prompt store agent.
2. **Resilient JSON Block Extraction:** Replace the brittle `jq` extraction line in the bash script with a regex-powered python parser that extracts the outer `{...}` JSON block regardless of any header logs, separation banners, or python warnings in the buffer.

### 🛠️ Step-by-Step Fix

Run the following commands in your workspace to apply the fixes and re-run Step 6 verification:

```bash

# Apply cleanups to both python and bash files
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
import re

# 1. Update datetime handling in agents/gcs_prompt_store.py
path_agent = Path("agents/gcs_prompt_store.py")
if path_agent.exists():
    code = path_agent.read_text()
    # Safely swap naive datetime for timezone-aware utc datetime
    code = code.replace("from datetime import datetime", "from datetime import datetime, timezone")
    code = code.replace("datetime.utcnow()", "datetime.now(timezone.utc)")
    path_agent.write_text(code)
    print("✓ Updated agents/gcs_prompt_store.py to timezone-aware datetime.")

# 2. Add bulletproof JSON extraction to scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh
path_script = Path("scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh")
if path_script.exists():
    content = path_script.read_text()
    old_line = 'RUN_ID=$(echo "$METADATA_JSON" | jq -r \'.run_id\')'
    new_line = 'RUN_ID=$(echo "$METADATA_JSON" | python3 -c "import sys, json, re; m=re.search(r\'(\\{.*\\})\', sys.stdin.read(), re.DOTALL); print(json.loads(m.group(1))[\'run_id\'])" 2>/dev/null || echo "")'
    
    if old_line in content:
        content = content.replace(old_line, new_line)
        path_script.write_text(content)
        print("✓ Updated scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh with resilient JSON extraction.")
    else:
        # Fallback matching pattern in case formatting differed slightly
        updated, count = re.subn(r'RUN_ID=\$\(echo\s+"\$METADATA_JSON"\s*\|\s*jq\s+-r\s+\'\.run_id\'\)', new_line, content)
        if count > 0:
            path_script.write_text(updated)
            print("✓ Updated scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh using regex match.")
        else:
            print("⚠️ scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh might already be updated or structured differently.")
PY

---

### LOCKED: Metadata Model

```
prompt_uid = enterprise primary key
 Example: vertexai:3381323161097207808

source_prompt_id = source traceability
 Example: 3381323161097207808

source_system = multi-platform support
 Values: vertexai, openai, anthropic, xai, ossa, prism
```

**Reference:** PHASE_1_5_METADATA_LAKE.md (Governance Document)

---

### LOCKED: Versioning Model (SCD Type 2)

```
version_number    → INT64 (incrementing per prompt_uid)
parent_run_id    → STRING UUID (previous version)
valid_from      → TIMESTAMP (when version became current)
valid_to       → TIMESTAMP (when superseded)
is_current      → BOOL (TRUE only for latest)
```

**Rules:**
- Previous version: `is_current=FALSE`, `valid_to=NOW()`
- New version: `is_current=TRUE`, `valid_from=NOW()`, `valid_to=NULL`
- Never delete previous versions
- Never overwrite previous versions

---

### LOCKED: Audit Model

```
prompt_events table (mandatory)

Fields:
 event_id    → STRING UUID
 prompt_uid   → STRING
 version_number → INT64
 run_id     → STRING UUID
 event_type   → STRING (enum below)
 lifecycle_status → STRING (enum below)
 severity    → STRING (info|warning|error)
 message     → STRING
 created_at   → TIMESTAMP
```

**Rules:**
- Every status change = event
- Every operation = event
- Complete audit trail required

---

### LOCKED: UUID Strategy

Every entity gets UUID v4:

```
run_id       → Extraction run identifier
chunk_id      → Individual chunk identifier (NOT chunk_001.md)
attachment_id    → File attachment identifier
event_id      → Lifecycle event identifier
```

**Rules:**
- Use UUID, not filename
- Use `chunk_order` INT for reconstruction
- Sort by `chunk_order`, not by name

---

### LOCKED: Lifecycle Status Values

```
created       → Extraction initialized
extracting      → Extraction in progress
bronze_completed   → Raw layer done
silver_completed   → Structured layer done
gold_completed    → Knowledge layer done
completed      → Entire extraction done
skipped_unchanged  → Hash matched, no extraction
failed        → Error occurred
```

**Rules:**
- Follow progression: created → extracting → bronze_completed → silver_completed → gold_completed → completed
- Or: skipped_unchanged (no version created)
- Or: failed (with error details)

---

### LOCKED: Repeat Modes

```
first_run      → Initial extraction
changed_new_version → Hash differs, create v2
force_new_version  → --force flag, create new version
unchanged_skip    → Hash matches, skip extraction
```

**Rules:**
- Auto-detected by comparing hashes
- Determines if new run_id and version_number created
- Logged in prompt_events

---

### Deliverable 3: Lifecycle State Machine

```
created
  ↓
extracting (insert event)
  ↓
bronze_completed (insert event)
  ↓
silver_completed (insert event)
  ↓
gold_completed (insert event)
  ↓
completed (insert event)
```

**Error Paths:**
```
Any status → failed (insert event with error message)
```

**Skip Path:**
```
extracting → skipped_unchanged (insert event, NO new version)
```

**Requirements:**
- Track state in `lifecycle_status` field
- Insert event for EVERY transition
- Never skip event logging
- Distinguish between terminal and transient states

### Deliverable 4: Hash-Based Change Detection

**Implement:** In gcs_prompt_store.py

**Logic:**

```python
raw_hash = MD5(JSON(raw_data, sorted=True))
previous_hash = query_bigquery(prompt_uid)

if previous_hash == raw_hash and not --force:
  # No change detected
  repeat_mode = "unchanged_skip"
  lifecycle_status = "skipped_unchanged"
  insert_event(event_type="skipped_unchanged")
  return (no new version, no new run_id)
else:
  # Change detected (or forced)
  repeat_mode = "changed_new_version" or "force_new_version"
  create_new_run_id()
  increment_version_number()
  set_parent_run_id()
  return (new version, new run_id)
```

**Requirements:**
- Compute MD5 on raw JSON (deterministic)
- Compare to previous version
- Skip extraction if unchanged (save API calls)
- Create event for skip
- Support --force flag

---

### Deliverable 5: Version Lineage Tracking

**Implement:** In bigquery_prompt_catalog.py

**When hash changes or --force:**

```sql
-- Close previous version
UPDATE prompt_versions
SET is_current = FALSE, valid_to = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
WHERE prompt_uid = @prompt_uid
 AND version_number = @previous_version
 AND is_current = TRUE;

-- Insert new version
INSERT INTO prompt_versions (
 prompt_uid, version_number, parent_run_id,
 is_current, valid_from, valid_to,
 ...
) VALUES (
 @prompt_uid, @new_version, @previous_run_id,
 TRUE, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), NULL,
 ...
);

-- Insert lineage event
INSERT INTO prompt_events (
 event_id, prompt_uid, version_number, run_id,
 event_type, repeat_mode, lifecycle_status
) VALUES (
 @event_id, @prompt_uid, @new_version, @new_run_id,
 "version_created", @repeat_mode, "created"
);
```

**Requirements:**
- parent_run_id points to previous version's run_id
- Enables lineage queries: `WITH RECURSIVE parent_chain AS ...`
- Never lose version history
- Track repeat_mode for audit trail

#### Test 5: Lineage Query

```sql
WITH RECURSIVE lineage AS (
 SELECT
  prompt_uid, version_number, run_id, parent_run_id,
  is_current, valid_from, valid_to
 FROM ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_versions
 WHERE prompt_uid = 'vertexai:3381323161097207808'
  AND is_current = TRUE
  
 UNION ALL
  
 SELECT
  pv.prompt_uid, pv.version_number, pv.run_id, pv.parent_run_id,
  pv.is_current, pv.valid_from, pv.valid_to
 FROM ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_versions pv
 INNER JOIN lineage l ON pv.run_id = l.parent_run_id
)
SELECT * FROM lineage ORDER BY version_number DESC;
```

**Expected:**
- Full chain: v3 → v2 → v1
- Each row shows parent relationship
- valid_from/valid_to show when each was current
- is_current shows only v3=TRUE, others FALSE

## IMPLEMENTATION NOTES

### Hash Computation

```python
import hashlib
import json

raw_hash = hashlib.md5(
  json.dumps(raw_data, sort_keys=True, separators=(',', ':')).encode()
).hexdigest()
```

Deterministic: Same data = same hash always.

### UUID Generation

```python
import uuid

run_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
chunk_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
attachment_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
event_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
```

### SCD Type 2 Insert

```sql
-- Close previous
UPDATE prompt_versions
SET is_current = FALSE, valid_to = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
WHERE prompt_uid = @uid AND is_current = TRUE;

-- Open new
INSERT INTO prompt_versions (
 prompt_uid, version_number, parent_run_id,
 is_current, valid_from, valid_to, ...
) VALUES (
 @uid, @new_version, @prev_run_id,
 TRUE, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), NULL, ...
);
```

### Event Insertion

```python
# For each lifecycle status change
insert_event(
  event_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
  prompt_uid=prompt_uid,
  version_number=version_number,
  run_id=run_id,
  event_type="bronze_completed",
  lifecycle_status="bronze_completed",
  severity="info",
  message="Bronze layer: raw.json uploaded",
  created_at=datetime.utcnow()
)
```

[USER] #!/bin/bash
# Extract and Store Prompt in GCS + BigQuery Catalog
# Usage: ./scripts/extract_store_prompt.sh <prompt_id> [--force]

set -euo pipefail

SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
PROJECT_ROOT="$(cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/.." && pwd)"

PROMPT_ID="${1:?ERROR: prompt_id required}"
FORCE="${2:-}"

METADATA_JSON=$(python3 agents/gcs_prompt_store.py \
 --prompt-id "$PROMPT_ID" \
 --project-id "ctoteam" \
 --location "us-central1" \
 --bucket "agentproject" \
 $([[ -n "$FORCE" ]] && echo "--force") 2>&1 | tail -50)

# Extract run_id from metadata

if [[ -z "$RUN_ID" || "$RUN_ID" == "null" ]]; then
 echo "ERROR: Failed to extract run_id from metadata"
 exit 1-- BigQuery Schema for PRISM Prompt Catalog

-- Stores metadata and indexes for prompt extractions in GCS

OPTIONS(
 description="PRISM prompt extraction catalog with GCS artifact registry",
 location="US"
);

-- Table 1: Prompt Runs (one row per extraction)
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_runs` (
 prompt_id STRING NOT NULL,
 run_id STRING NOT NULL,
 raw_hash STRING NOT NULL,
 extracted_hash STRING NOT NULL,
 status STRING NOT NULL, -- success | failed | processing
 latest BOOL NOT NULL,
 created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
 gcs_run_uri STRING NOT NULL, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
 gcs_latest_uri STRING, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/latest.json
 chunk_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 system_present BOOL NOT NULL,
 user_message_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 model_message_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 text_attachment_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 binary_attachment_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 raw_size_bytes INT64 NOT NULL,
 extracted_chars INT64 NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(created_at)
CLUSTER BY prompt_id, latest, status;

-- Table 2: Prompt Chunks (one row per chunk within a run)
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_chunks` (
 prompt_id STRING NOT NULL,
 run_id STRING NOT NULL,
 chunk_id STRING NOT NULL, -- UUID
 chunk_order INT64 NOT NULL, -- 0-indexed chunk number
 chunk_file STRING NOT NULL, -- chunk_001.md, etc
 gcs_uri STRING NOT NULL, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/chunks/chunk_001.md
 char_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 estimated_tokens INT64 NOT NULL, -- ~4 chars = 1 token
 rompt_catalog`
OPTIONS(
 description="PRISM prompt extraction catalog with GCS artifact registry",
 location="US"
);

-- Table 1: Prompt Runs (one row per extraction)
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_runs` (
 prompt_id STRING NOT NULL,
 run_id STRING NOT NULL,
 raw_hash STRING NOT NULL,
 extracted_hash STRING NOT NULL,
 status STRING NOT NULL, -- success | failed | processing
 latest BOOL NOT NULL,
 created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
 gcs_run_uri STRING NOT NULL, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
 gcs_latest_uri STRING, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/latest.json
 chunk_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 system_present BOOL NOT NULL,
 user_message_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 model_message_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 text_attachment_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 binary_attachment_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 raw_size_bytes INT64 NOT NULL,
 extracted_chars INT64 NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(created_at)
CLUSTER BY prompt_id, latest, status;

-- Table 2: Prompt Chunks (one row per chunk within a run)
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_chunks` (
 prompt_id STRING NOT NULL,
 run_id STRING NOT NULL,
 chunk_id STRING NOT NULL, -- UUID
 chunk_order INT64 NOT NULL, -- 0-indexed chunk number
 chunk_file STRING NOT NULL, -- chunk_001.md, etc
 gcs_uri STRING NOT NULL, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/chunks/chunk_001.md
 char_count INT64 NOT NULL,
 estimated_tokens INT64 NOT NULL, -- ~4 chars = 1 token
 role STRING NOT NULL, -- system | user | model
 artifact_type STRING NOT NULL, -- text | code | markdown
 created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(created_at)
CLUSTER BY prompt_id, run_id, chunk_order;

-- Table 3: Prompt Attachments (images, PDFs, files)
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_attachments` (
 prompt_id STRING NOT NULL,
 run_id STRING NOT NULL,
 attachment_id STRING NOT NULL, -- UUID
 mime_type STRING NOT NULL, -- image/png, application/pdf, text/plain, etc
 attachment_type STRING NOT NULL, -- image | pdf | text | binary
 local_path STRING, -- path before upload (reference only)
 gcs_uri STRING NOT NULL, -- gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/attachments/<attachment_id>
 size_bytes INT64 NOT NULL,
 decoded BOOL NOT NULL, -- true if text/plain was base64 decoded
 created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(created_at)
CLUSTER BY prompt_id, run_id, attachment_type;

-- View: Latest Run per Prompt
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.latest_runs` AS
SELECT
 prompt_id,
 run_id,
 raw_hash,
 extracted_hash,
 status,
 created_at,
 gcs_run_uri,
 chunk_count,
 user_message_count,
 model_message_count,
 text_attachment_count,
 binary_attachment_count
FROM
 `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_runs`
WHERE
 latest = TRUE
ORDER BY
 prompt_id, created_at DESC;

-- View: Extraction Status Summary
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.extraction_status` AS
SELECT
 prompt_id,
 COUNT(DISTINCT run_id) as total_runs,
 COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN status = 'success' THEN run_id END) as successful_runs,
 COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN status = 'failed' THEN run_id END) as failed_runs,
 MAX(created_at) as last_extraction,
 ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT raw_hash IGNORE NULLS) as raw_hashes,
 ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT extracted_hash IGNORE NULLS) as extracted_hashes
FROM
 `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_runs`
GROUP BY
 prompt_id;

-- View: Chunk Distribution
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.chunk_distribution` AS
SELECT
 prompt_id,
 run_id,
 COUNT(*) as chunk_count,
 SUM(char_count) as total_chars,
 SUM(estimated_tokens) as total_tokens,
 ROUND(AVG(char_count), 0) as avg_chunk_chars,
 MIN(char_count) as min_chunk_chars,
 MAX(char_count) as max_chunk_chars,
 ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT role) as roles,
 ARRAY_AGG(DISTINCT artifact_type) as artifact_types
FROM
 `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_chunks`
GROUP BY
 prompt_id, run_id;


fi

echo "✓ Uploaded to GCS (run_id: ${RUN_ID:0:8}...)"

# STAGE 2: Register in BigQuery

 #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
GCS Prompt Store Agent

Extracts Vertex AI saved prompts and stores artifacts in Google Cloud Storage.
Organized by prompt_id and run_id (UUID). Immutable run folders.

Flow:
1. Fetch prompt from Vertex AI Dataset API
2. Extract: system, user messages, attachments (deterministic, no LLM)
3. Create local run folder: saved_prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
4. Upload entire run folder to: gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/<prompt_id>/runs/<run_id>/
5. Update latest.json pointer
6. Return metadata for BigQuery registration
"""

import sys
import json
import subprocess
import requests
import base64
import argparse
import hashlib
import uuid
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
from google.cloud import storage

def get_auth_token() -> str:
  """Get GCP access token."""
  try:
    return subprocess.check_output(
      ["gcloud", "auth", "print-access-token"], text=True
    ).strip()
  except:
    try:
      return subprocess.check_output(
        ["gcloud", "auth", "application-default", "print-access-token"], text=True
      ).strip()
    except:
      print("ERROR: gcloud auth failed. Run: gcloud auth login --no-launch-browser")
      sys.exit(1)


def compute_md5(data: dict) -> str:
  """Compute MD5 hash of JSON (deterministic)."""
  json_str = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True, separators=(',', ':'))
  return hashlib.md5(json_str.encode()).hexdigest()


def fetch_prompt(project_id: str, location: str, prompt_id: str, token: str) -> dict:
  """Fetch saved prompt from Vertex AI Dataset API."""
  url = f"https://{location}-aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/{project_id}/locations/{location}/datasets/{prompt_id}"
  headers = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {token}",
    "x-goog-user-project": project_id,
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
  }

  r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=30)
  if r.status_code != 200:
    raise RuntimeError(f"Fetch failed {r.status_code}: {r.text}")

  return r.json()


def decode_base64_text(b64_str: str) -> str:
  """Decode base64 text, return original if fails."""
  try:
    return base64.b64decode(b64_str).decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
  except:
    return f"[Decode failed: {b64_str[:50]}...]"


def clean_node(node: any) -> any:
  """Recursively clean JSON: decode text/plain, strip binary payloads."""
  if isinstance(node, dict):
    has_mime = any(k in node for k in ["mime_type", "mimeType", "mime"])
    if "data" in node and has_mime:
      mime = node.get("mime_type") or node.get("mimeType") or node.get("mime") or ""
      raw_data = node["data"]
      if mime == "text/plain" and raw_data:
        node["data"] = decode_base64_text(raw_data)
      else:
        size = len(raw_data) if raw_data else 0
        node["data"] = f"<stripped_payload:{mime}:{size}_bytes>"

    for k, v in list(node.items()):
      if k == "text" and isinstance(v, str):
        try:
          nested = json.loads(v)
          node[k] = json.dumps(clean_node(nested))
        except:
          pass
      else:
        node[k] = clean_node(v)
  elif isinstance(node, list):
    return [clean_node(item) for item in node]

  return node


def extract_prompt_structure(cleaned_data: dict) -> Tuple[str, List[str], List[dict]]:
  """
  Extract system instruction, user messages, and attachments from cleaned JSON.
  Returns: (system_instruction_text, user_messages_list, attachments_list)
  """
  system_instruction = ""
  user_messages = []
  attachments = []

  def parse_prompt_message(msg):
    nonlocal system_instruction

    # Extract system instruction
    sys_inst = msg.get("systemInstruction", {}) or msg.get("system_instruction", {})
    if sys_inst:
      parts = sys_inst.get("parts", [])
      system_instruction = "\n".join([p.get("text", "") for p in parts if "text" in p])

    # Extract user/model messages and attachments
    for content in msg.get("contents", []):
      role = content.get("role", "user")
      if role in ("user", "model", None):
        for part in content.get("parts", []):
          if "text" in part:
            user_messages.append({
              "role": role or "user",
              "type": "text",
              "content": part["text"]
            })
          elif "inline_data" in part or "inlineData" in part:
            data_obj = part.get("inline_data") or part.get("inlineData", {})
            mime = data_obj.get("mime_type") or data_obj.get("mimeType", "")
            raw_data = data_obj.get("data", "")

            attachment_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
            attachments.append({
              "id": attachment_id,
              "mime_type": mime,
              "role": role or "user",
              "size_bytes": len(raw_data) if raw_data else 0,
              "decoded": False
            })

            # If text/plain, also add as message
            if mime == "text/plain" and raw_data:
              decoded = decode_base64_text(raw_data)
              user_messages.append({
                "role": role or "user",
                "type": "attachment",
                "content": decoded,
                "attachment_id": attachment_id,
                "mime_type": mime
              })

  # Parse metadata.text
  metadata = cleaned_data.get("metadata", {})
  text_str = metadata.get("text", "")
  if text_str:
    try:
      text_json = json.loads(text_str)
      prompt_message = text_json.get("structured_prompt", {}).get("prompt_message", {})
      if prompt_message:
        parse_prompt_message(prompt_message)
    except:
      pass

  # Fallback to promptApiSchema
  if not user_messages and not system_instruction:
    prompt_api_schema = cleaned_data.get("promptApiSchema", {})
    prompt_message = prompt_api_schema.get("multimodalPrompt", {}).get("promptMessage", {})
    if not prompt_message:
      prompt_message = prompt_api_schema.get("promptMessage", {})
    if prompt_message:
      parse_prompt_message(prompt_message)

  return system_instruction, user_messages, attachments


def create_run_folder(prompt_id: str, run_id: str,
           raw_data: dict, cleaned_data: dict,
           system_instruction: str, user_messages: List[dict],
           attachments: List[dict]) -> Path:
  """Create local run folder with all extracted content."""
  run_dir = Path(f"saved_prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}")
  run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

  # Save raw data
  (run_dir / "raw.json").write_text(json.dumps(raw_data, indent=2))
  (run_dir / "raw_clean.json").write_text(json.dumps(cleaned_data, indent=2))

  # Save system instruction
  if system_instruction:
    (run_dir / "system.md").write_text(f"# System Instruction\n\n{system_instruction}\n")

  # Save user messages grouped by role
  (run_dir / "user_messages").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
  for i, msg in enumerate(user_messages, 1):
    role = msg.get("role", "user")
    content = msg.get("content", "")
    (run_dir / "user_messages" / f"{i:03d}_{role}.txt").write_text(content)

  # Save attachments
  (run_dir / "attachments").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
  for att in attachments:
    att_file = run_dir / "attachments" / f"{att['id']}.json"
    att_file.write_text(json.dumps(att, indent=2))

  # Create chunks (deterministic)
  extracted_text = f"=== SYSTEM ===\n{system_instruction}\n\n=== USER ===\n"
  extracted_text += "\n\n".join([msg.get("content", "") for msg in user_messages])

  chunks = []
  chunk_size = 15000
  overlap = 1500
  start = 0
  while start < len(extracted_text):
    end = min(start + chunk_size, len(extracted_text))
    chunks.append(extracted_text[start:end])
    if end >= len(extracted_text):
      break
    start = end - overlap

  (run_dir / "chunks").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
  chunk_files = []
  for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks, 1):
    chunk_file = f"chunk_{i:03d}.md"
    (run_dir / "chunks" / chunk_file).write_text(chunk)
    chunk_files.append(chunk_file)

  # Create master & assembled
  master = f"# Prompt {prompt_id}\n\n- **Run ID:** {run_id}\n- **Chunks:** {len(chunks)}\n\n"
  for cf in chunk_files:
    master += f"- `{cf}`\n"
  (run_dir / "master.md").write_text(master)

  final = master + f"\n{'='*60}\n# CONTENT\n\n" + "\n\n".join(chunks)
  (run_dir / "final_assembled.md").write_text(final)

  # Create extraction report
  report = {
    "prompt_id": prompt_id,
    "run_id": run_id,
    "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat() + "Z",
    "chunk_count": len(chunks),
    "user_message_count": len(user_messages),
    "model_message_count": sum(1 for m in user_messages if m.get("role") == "model"),
    "text_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "binary_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if not a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "raw_size_bytes": len(json.dumps(raw_data)),
    "extracted_chars": len(extracted_text),
    "system_present": bool(system_instruction),
  }
  (run_dir / "extraction_report.json").write_text(json.dumps(report, indent=2))

  return run_dir


def upload_to_gcs(run_dir: Path, bucket_name: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str) -> str:
  """Upload run folder to GCS."""
  client = storage.Client()
  bucket = client.bucket(bucket_name)

  gcs_prefix = f"saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}"

  for file_path in run_dir.rglob("*"):
    if file_path.is_file():
      rel_path = file_path.relative_to(run_dir)
      gcs_path = f"{gcs_prefix}/{rel_path}".replace("\\", "/")

      blob = bucket.blob(gcs_path)
      blob.upload_from_filename(file_path)

  return f"gs://{bucket_name}/{gcs_prefix}/"


def update_latest_pointer(bucket_name: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str) -> str:
  """Update latest.json pointer."""
  client = storage.Client()
  bucket = client.bucket(bucket_name)

  latest_data = {
    "prompt_id": prompt_id,
    "latest_run_id": run_id,
    "updated_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat() + "Z",
    "gcs_uri": f"gs://{bucket_name}/saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}/"
  }

  blob = bucket.blob(f"saved-prompts/{": sum(1 for m in user_messages if m.get("role") == "model"),
    "text_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "binary_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if not a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "raw_size_bytes": len(json.dumps(raw_data)),
    "extracted_chars": len(extracted_text),
    "system_present": bool(system_instruction),
  }
  (run_dir / "extraction_report.json").write_text(json.dumps(report, indent=2))

  return run_dir


def upload_to_gcs(run_dir: Path, bucket_name: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str) -> str:
  """Upload run folder to GCS."""
  client = storage.Client()
  bucket = client.bucket(bucket_name)

  gcs_prefix = f"saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}"

  for file_path in run_dir.rglob("*"):
    if file_path.is_file():
      rel_path = file_path.relative_to(run_dir)
      gcs_path = f"{gcs_prefix}/{rel_path}".replace("\\", "/")

      blob = bucket.blob(gcs_path)
      blob.upload_from_filename(file_path)

  return f"gs://{bucket_name}/{gcs_prefix}/"


def update_latest_pointer(bucket_name: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str) -> str:
  """Update latest.json pointer."""
  client = storage.Client()
  bucket = client.bucket(bucket_name)

  latest_data = {
    "prompt_id": prompt_id,
    "latest_run_id": run_id,
    "updated_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat() + "Z",
    "gcs_uri": f"gs://{bucket_name}/saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}/"
  }

  blob = bucket.blob(f"saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/latest.json")
  blob.upload_from_string(json.dumps(latest_data, indent=2), content_type="application/json")

  return f"gs://{bucket_name}/saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/latest.json"


def main():
  parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="GCS Prompt Store Agent")
  parser.add_argument("--prompt-id", required=True)
  parser.add_argument("--project-id", default="ctoteam")
  parser.add_argument("--location", default="us-central1")
  parser.add_argument("--bucket", default="agentproject")
  parser.add_argument("--force", action="store_true")

  args = parser.parse_args()

  print(f"\n{'='*70}")
  print(f"GCS PROMPT STORE AGENT")
  print(f"{'='*70}")
  print(f"Prompt ID: {args.prompt_id}")
  print(f"Project: {args.project_id}")
  print(f"GCS Bucket: gs://{args.bucket}/")

  token = get_auth_token()

  # STAGE 1: Fetch
  print(f"\n[STAGE 1] Fetching Prompt")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")
  raw_data = fetch_prompt(args.project_id, args.location, args.prompt_id, token)
  raw_hash = compute_md5(raw_data)
  print(f"✓ Fetched (hash: {raw_hash[:8]}...)")

  # STAGE 2: Clean & Extract
  print(f"\n[STAGE 2] Extracting Content")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")
  cleaned_data = clean_node(raw_data)
  system_instruction, user_messages, attachments = extract_prompt_structure(cleaned_data)
  extracted_hash = hashlib.md5((system_instruction + "".join(m.get("content", "") for m in user_messages)).encode()).hexdigest()
  print(f"✓ System: {bool(system_instruction)} | Messages: {len(user_messages)} | Attachments: {len(attachments)}")
  print(f"✓ Extracted hash: {extracted_hash[:8]}...")

  # STAGE 3: Create local run folder
  print(f"\n[STAGE 3] Creating Local Run Folder")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")
  run_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
  run_dir = create_run_folder(
    args.prompt_id, run_id, raw_data, cleaned_data,
    system_instruction, user_messages, attachments
  )
  print(f"✓ Run ID: {run_id}")
  print(f"✓ Local folder: {run_dir}")

  # STAGE 4: Upload to GCS
  print(f"\n[STAGE 4] Uploading to GCS")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")
  gcs_uri = upload_to_gcs(run_dir, args.bucket, args.prompt_id, run_id)
  print(f"✓ Uploaded: {gcs_uri}")

  # STAGE 5: Update latest pointer
  print(f"\n[STAGE 5] Updating Latest Pointer")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")
  latest_uri = update_latest_pointer(args.bucket, args.prompt_id, run_id)
  print(f"✓ Latest: {latest_uri}")

  # Return metadata for BigQuery
  metadata = {
    "prompt_id": args.prompt_id,
    "run_id": run_id,
    "raw_hash": raw_hash,
    "extracted_hash": extracted_hash,
    "status": "success",
    "gcs_run_uri": gcs_uri,
    "gcs_latest_uri": latest_uri,
    "chunk_count": len([f for f in run_dir.rglob("chunk_*.md")]),
    "system_present": bool(system_instruction),
    "user_message_count": len(user_messages),
    "model_message_count": sum(1 for m in user_messages if m.get("role") == "model"),
    "text_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "binary_attachment_count": sum(1 for a in attachments if not a["mime_type"].startswith("text")),
    "raw_size_bytes": len(json.dumps(raw_data)),
    "extracted_chars": len(system_instruction) + sum(len(m.get("content", "")) for m in user_messages),
  }

  print(f"\n{'='*70}")
  print(f"EXTRACTION & UPLOAD COMPLETE")
  print(f"{'='*70}")
  print(json.dumps(metadata, indent=2))


if __name__ == "__main__":
  main()

[USER] #!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
BigQuery Prompt Catalog Agent

Registers prompt extraction metadata in BigQuery after GCS upload.
Maintains searchable catalog of all prompt extractions.

Input: Metadata dict from gcs_prompt_store.py
Output: BigQuery records, queryable catalog
"""

import sys
import json
import argparse
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from google.cloud import bigquery
from pathlib import Path


def register_prompt_run(project_id: str, metadata: dict) -> bool:
  """Register prompt run in BigQuery."""
  client = bigquery.Client(project=project_id)

  dataset_id = "prism_prompt_catalog"
  table_id = "prompt_runs"

  rows_to_insert = [
    {
      "prompt_id": metadata["prompt_id"],
      "run_id": metadata["run_id"],
      "raw_hash": metadata["raw_hash"],
      "extracted_hash": metadata["extracted_hash"],
      "status": metadata.get("status", "success"),
      "latest": True, # Mark as latest (will unset others)
      "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
      "gcs_run_uri": metadata["gcs_run_uri"],
      "gcs_latest_uri": metadata.get("gcs_latest_uri"),
      "chunk_count": metadata["chunk_count"],
      "system_present": metadata["system_present"],
      "user_message_count": metadata["user_message_count"],
      "model_message_count": metadata["model_message_count"],
      "text_attachment_count": metadata["text_attachment_count"],
      "binary_attachment_count": metadata["binary_attachment_count"],
      "raw_size_bytes": metadata["raw_size_bytes"],
      "extracted_chars": metadata["extracted_chars"],
    }
  ]

  table = client.get_table(f"{project_id}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}")
  errors = client.insert_rows_json(table, rows_to_insert)

  if errors:
    print(f"ERROR inserting rows: {errors}")
    return False

  # Unset latest flag for previous runs
  query = f"""
  UPDATE `{project_id}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}`
  SET latest = FALSE
  WHERE prompt_id = @prompt_id
   AND run_id != @run_id
   AND latest = TRUE;
  """

  job_config = bigquery.QueryJobConfig(
    query_parameters=[
      bigquery.ScalarQueryParameter("prompt_id", "STRING", metadata["prompt_id"]),
      bigquery.ScalarQueryParameter("run_id", "STRING", metadata["run_id"]),
    ]
  )

  client.query(query, job_config=job_config).result()

  return True


def register_chunks(project_id: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str, chunks_dir: Path) -> bool:
  """Register chunks in BigQuery."""
  client = bigquery.Client(project=project_id)

  dataset_id = "prism_prompt_catalog"
  table_id = "prompt_chunks"

  rows_to_insert = []
  chunk_files = sorted(chunks_dir.glob("chunk_*.md"))

  for chunk_order, chunk_file in enumerate(chunk_files):
    content = chunk_file.read_text()
    char_count = len(content)
    estimated_tokens = max(1, char_count // 4)

    rows_to_insert.append({
      "prompt_id": prompt_id,
      "run_id": run_id,
      "chunk_id": str(chunk_file.stem),
      "chunk_order": chunk_order,
      "chunk_file": chunk_file.name,
      "gcs_uri": f"gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}/chunks/{chunk_file.name}",
      "char_count": char_count,
      "estimated_tokens": estimated_tokens,
      "role": "system|user",
      "artifact_type": "markdown",
      "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
    })

  if not rows_to_insert:
    return True

  table = client.get_table(f"{project_id}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}")
  errors = client.insert_rows_json(table, rows_to_insert)

  if errors:
    print(f"ERROR inserting chunks: {errors}")
    return False

  return True


def register_attachments(project_id: str, prompt_id: str, run_id: str,
            attachments_dir: Path) -> bool:
  """Register attachments in BigQuery."""
  client = bigquery.Client(project=project_id)

  dataset_id = "prism_prompt_catalog"
  table_id = "prompt_attachments"

  rows_to_insert = []
  att_files = list(attachments_dir.glob("*.json"))

  for att_file in att_files:
    att_data = json.loads(att_file.read_text())

    mime_type = att_data.get("mime_type", "unknown")
    if mime_type.startswith("image"):
      att_type = "image"
    elif mime_type.startswith("application/pdf"):
      att_type = "pdf"
    elif mime_type.startswith("text"):
      att_type = "text"
    else:
      att_type = "binary"

    rows_to_insert.append({
      "prompt_id": prompt_id,
      "run_id": run_id,
      "attachment_id": att_data.get("id"),
      "mime_type": mime_type,
      "attachment_type": att_type,
      "local_path": att_file.name,
      "gcs_uri": f"gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/{prompt_id}/runs/{run_id}/attachments/{att_file.name}",
      "size_bytes": att_data.get("size_bytes", 0),
      "decoded": att_data.get("decoded", False),
      "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
    })

  if not rows_to_insert:
    return True

  table = client.get_table(f"{project_id}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}")
  errors = client.insert_rows_json(table, rows_to_insert)

  if errors:
    print(f"ERROR inserting attachments: {errors}")
    return False

  return True


def query_latest_runs(project_id: str) -> list:
  """Query latest runs."""
  client = bigquery.Client(project=project_id)

  query = """
  SELECT
   prompt_id,
   run_id,
   raw_hash,
   extracted_hash,
   created_at,
   gcs_run_uri,
   chunk_count,
   user_message_count,
   text_attachment_count,
   binary_attachment_count
  FROM `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.latest_runs`
  ORDER BY created_at DESC
  LIMIT 10;
  """

  results = client.query(query).result()
  return [dict(row) for row in results]


def main():
  parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="BigQuery Prompt Catalog Agent")
  parser.add_argument("--prompt-id", required=True)
  parser.add_argument("--run-id", required=True)
  parser.add_argument("--project-id", default="ctoteam")
  parser.add_argument("--metadata-file", help="JSON file with metadata dict")
  parser.add_argument("--run-folder", help="Path to run folder for chunk/attachment registration")

  args = parser.parse_args()

  print(f"\n{'='*70}")
  print(f"BIGQUERY PROMPT CATALOG AGENT")
  print(f"{'='*70}")

  # Load metadata
  if args.metadata_file:
    metadata = json.loads(Path(args.metadata_file).read_text())
  else:
    metadata = {
      "prompt_id": args.prompt_id,
      "run_id": args.run_id,
      "raw_hash": "unknown",
      "extracted_hash": "unknown",
      "status": "unknown",
      "gcs_run_uri": f"gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/{args.prompt_id}/runs/{args.run_id}/",
      "chunk_count": 0,
      "system_present": False,
      "user_message_count": 0,
      "model_message_count": 0,
      "text_attachment_count": 0,
      "binary_attachment_count": 0,
      "raw_size_bytes": 0,
      "extracted_chars": 0,
    }

  print(f"\n[STAGE 1] Registering Prompt Run")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")

  if not register_prompt_run(args.project_id, metadata):
    print("ERROR registering prompt run")
    sys.exit(1)

  print(f"✓ Registered: {metadata['prompt_id']}/{metadata['run_id']}")

  # Register chunks if run folder provided
  if args.run_folder:
    run_dir = Path(args.run_folder)
    chunks_dir = run_dir / "chunks"

    if chunks_dir.exists():
      print(f"\n[STAGE 2] Registering Chunks")
      print(f"{'-'*70}")

      if not register_chunks(args.project_id, args.prompt_id, args.run_id, chunks_dir):
        print("ERROR registering chunks")
        sys.exit(1)

      print(f"✓ Registered {len(list(chunks_dir.glob('*.md')))} chunks")

    # Register attachments if present
    att_dir = run_dir / "attachments"
    if att_dir.exists():
      print(f"\n[STAGE 3] Registering Attachments")
      print(f"{'-'*70}")

      if not register_attachments(args.project_id, args.prompt_id, args.run_id, att_dir):
        print("ERROR registering attachments")
        sys.exit(1)

      print(f"✓ Registered {len(list(att_dir.glob('*.json')))} attachments")

  # Query catalog
  print(f"\n[STAGE 4] Querying Catalog")
  print(f"{'-'*70}")

  latest = query_latest_runs(args.project_id)
  print(f"✓ Latest {len(latest)} extractions:")
  for row in latest[:5]:
    print(f" - {row['prompt_id']}: {row['run_id'][:8]}... ({row['chunk_count']} chunks, {row['user_message_count']} msgs)")

  print(f"\n{'='*70}")
  print(f"REGISTRATION COMPLETE")
  print(f"{'='*70}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
  main()
