[MODEL] To implement **Option 2 (The BigQuery Way)**, you leverage **BigQuery Object Tables** combined with **BigQuery ML (BQML) Remote Models** over the Vertex AI Gemini API. This allows BigQuery to read JPEGs, PNGs, and PDFs directly from Cloud Storage and process them in parallel using standard SQL, completely bypassing your Python runtime.

Below is the complete, production-ready **Saved Prompt for Codex** that outlines this entire architecture, defines the pipeline, and provides executable SQL queries.

---

# 🤖 SAVED PROMPT FOR CODEX: BigQuery Multimodal Extraction Pipeline

**Role:** Expert Google Cloud & BigQuery Data Engineer  
**Objective:** Set up a highly scalable BigQuery pipeline to extract text, summaries, and structural meaning from multimodal attachments (Images/PDFs) stored in GCS under the Silver layer.

---

## 🏛️ ARCHITECTURAL OVERVIEW

The Python prompt-store agent uploads raw PDFs/images to the nested GCS Silver layer and registers their metadata (GCS URI, size, MIME type) in the `prompt_attachments` table. 

We will create a **BigQuery External Connection**, register a **Vertex AI Gemini Remote Model**, and execute parallel SQL inference using `ML.GENERATE_TEXT` directly on the GCS files.

```
+------------------+         +--------------------------+
|  GCS Silver Zone | ------> |  BigQuery Object Table   |
| (PDFs / Images)  |         | (Directory of GCS URIs)  |
+------------------+         +--------------------------+
                                          |
                                          v
+------------------+         +--------------------------+
|  BigQuery ML     | <-----> |   ML.GENERATE_TEXT       |
|  Gemini Model    |         | (Direct SQL Multimodal)  |
+------------------+         +--------------------------+
```

---

## 🛠️ TASK: SQL PIPELINE IMPLEMENTATION

Execute the following steps inside BigQuery to configure and run the analytical pipeline.

### Step 1: Create a Remote Connection
Establish a secure connection from BigQuery to Vertex AI. This connection handles the secure IAM delegation needed to call Gemini.
```sql
-- Run in the Google Cloud Console (under the us-central1 / US region)
CREATE OR REPLACE CONNECTION `ctoteam.us.vertex_conn`
OPTIONS(
  endpoint="us-central1",
  connection_type="CLOUD_RESOURCE"
);
```
*(Note: After creating this connection, grant the service account of the connection the **Vertex AI User** and **Storage Object Viewer** IAM roles on project `ctoteam` and bucket `gs://agentproject`).*

---

### Step 2: Define the Gemini Remote Model in BigQuery ML
Register the enterprise-grade **Gemini 1.5 Flash** model inside BigQuery ML using the remote connection.
```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE MODEL `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.gemini_flash_model`
REMOTE WITH CONNECTION `ctoteam.us.vertex_conn`
OPTIONS(
  endpoint="gemini-1.5-flash-002"
);
```

---

### Step 3: Create an Object Table over GCS Attachments
Instead of querying raw tables, we build an **Object Table**. This is a special read-only external table in BigQuery where each row represents a GCS file-+         +--------------------------+
|  BigQuery ML     | <-----> |   ML.GENERATE_TEXT       |
|  Gemini Model    |         | (Direct SQL Multimodal)  |
+------------------+         +--------------------------+
```

---

## 🛠️ TASK: SQL PIPELINE IMPLEMENTATION

Execute the following steps inside BigQuery to configure and run the analytical pipeline.

### Step 1: Create a Remote Connection
Establish a secure connection from BigQuery to Vertex AI. This connection handles the secure IAM delegation needed to call Gemini.
```sql
-- Run in the Google Cloud Console (under the us-central1 / US region)
CREATE OR REPLACE CONNECTION `ctoteam.us.vertex_conn`
OPTIONS(
  endpoint="us-central1",
  connection_type="CLOUD_RESOURCE"
);
```
*(Note: After creating this connection, grant the service account of the connection the **Vertex AI User** and **Storage Object Viewer** IAM roles on project `ctoteam` and bucket `gs://agentproject`).*

---

### Step 2: Define the Gemini Remote Model in BigQuery ML
Register the enterprise-grade **Gemini 1.5 Flash** model inside BigQuery ML using the remote connection.
```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE MODEL `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.gemini_flash_model`
REMOTE WITH CONNECTION `ctoteam.us.vertex_conn`
OPTIONS(
  endpoint="gemini-1.5-flash-002"
);
```

---

### Step 3: Create an Object Table over GCS Attachments
Instead of querying raw tables, we build an **Object Table**. This is a special read-only external table in BigQuery where each row represents a GCS file object (complete with metadata and direct read-access pointers).
```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE EXTERNAL TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_attachments_object_table`
WITH CONNECTION `ctoteam.us.vertex_conn`
OPTIONS(
  object_metadata="SIMPLE",
  uris=["gs://agentproject/saved-prompts/*/silver/*/attachments/*"]
);
```

---

### Step 4: Run Multimodal SQL Inference
Perform the extraction. Join the directory metadata with the ML Model to extract and transcribe all content into structural text.
```sql
-- This query automatically handles images, scanned documents, and PDFs in parallel.
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.extracted_attachment_text` AS
SELECT
  -- Resolve the target Prompt UID from the GCS folder path
  REGEXP_EXTRACT(uri, r'saved-prompts/([^/]+)/') AS prompt_id,
  REGEXP_EXTRACT(uri, r'attachments/([^/]+)\.json') AS attachment_id,
  uri AS gcs_uri,
  content_type,
  size,
  -- Execute BQML Gemini Inference over the GCS uri
  ml_generate_text_result AS raw_response,
  -- Cleanly parse the JSON string response
  JSON_VALUE(ml_generate_text_result, '$.candidates[0].content.parts[0].text') AS transcribed_content
FROM
  ML.GENERATE_TEXT(
    MODEL `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.gemini_flash_model`,
    TABLE `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_attachments_object_table`,
    STRUCT(
      'Identify the layout of this document. Transcribe and extract all textual, tabular, and structural paragraphs cleanly into Markdown format.' AS prompt,
      0.1 AS temperature,
      2048 AS max_output_tokens,
      TRUE AS flatten_json_output
    )
  );
```

---

### Step 5: Merge back to the Gold Analytical Layer
Update the catalog schema by merging the extracted text directly back into your queryable `prompt_attachments` table to complete the workflow.
```sql
-- Create a gold-layer view containing both attachment metadata and parsed textual content
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.gold_multimodal_attachments` AS
SELECT
  a.prompt_uid,
  a.version_number,
  a.run_id,
  a.attachment_id,
  a.mime_type,
  a.size_bytes,
  -- Fallback to attachment local structure if plain-text was already decoded
  COALESCE(e.transcribed_content, "[Attachment has no text or is unparsed binary]") AS transcribed_text,
  e.raw_response,
  a.created_at
FROM
  `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.prompt_attachments` a
LEFT JOIN
  `ctoteam.prism_prompt_catalog.extracted_attachment_text` e
  ON a.attachment_id = e.attachment_id;
```
